# UniSat Home | UniSat

[](https://docs.unisat.io/#welcome-to-unisat-documentation-hub)

Welcome to UniSat Documentation Hub


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the official UniSat Docs — your one-stop resource for exploring, building, and contributing within the UniSat ecosystem.

UniSat is a leading open-source wallet and service platform for Bitcoin Ordinals, brc-20, Runes, and Alkanes protocols.

Whether you’re here to understand our products, engage with the community, or dive into technical details — this is the place to start.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/#what-youll-find-in-the-unisat-documentation)

**What You'll Find in the UniSat Documentation:**

*   [**Products**](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet)
     Discover UniSat's core products, features, and user guides. Whether you’re trading on Marketplace, managing your wallet, or providing liquidity, the docs you need are here.
    
*   [**Community**](https://docs.unisat.io/community/unisat-points)
     Learn how to get involved, participate in events, explore the UniSat reputation system, and stay connected with the community. Discover resources, FAQs, and ways to actively engage with UniSat.
    
*   [**Devs**](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/open-api-documentation)
     In this section, developers can access a wide range of UniSat APIs, integration guides, and resources to create their own applications and tools within the UniSat ecosystem. Whether you're experimenting or building production-ready solutions, you’ll find the resources you need here.
    
*   [**Academy**](https://docs.unisat.io/academy/bitcoin)
     The Academy provides easy-to-understand educational content, tutorials, and guides to help you learn the basics and grow your understanding of the UniSat wallet.
    
*   [**Technical**](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/single-step-transfer)
     Explore detailed technical references, standards, and infrastructure components powering UniSat.
    

**Why UniSat Wallet?**

*   Your keys, your assets: A non-custodial design ensures you and you alone retain full control over your assets at all times.
    
*   Innovative and native: The first open-source wallet to fully support innovative standards on Bitcoin. Built by Bitcoiners, for Bitcoiners.
    
*   Trusted: Over 1 million users globally rely on UniSat to store their Bitcoin assets.
    
*   Seamless experience: Manage your portfolio, inscribe rare digital art and trade assets instantly - unlock the full Bitcoin experience in one seamless, secure interface.
    

Feel free to explore each section — whether you're a user, contributor, or developer, UniSat Docs hope to help you get started and stay informed.

UniSat Website:[https://unisat.io](https://unisat.io/)

UniScan:[https://uniscan.cc](https://uniscan.cc/)

PizzaSwap:[https://pizzaswap.io](https://pizzaswap.io/)

Open-API docs: [https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/unisat-open-api](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/unisat-open-api)

Open-API demonstration: [https://open-api.unisat.io/](https://open-api.unisat.io/)

# UniSat Work Priorities | UniSat

Welcome to UniSat’s Work Priorities page — a transparent, living overview of the core initiatives and focus development cycle.

This section outlines what we’re actively building, improving, or exploring. It reflects our evolving priorities as we grow the UniSat ecosystem, while staying responsive to community feedback and protocol-level changes.

What you'll find here: 🌱 Our goals

🛠️ Feature and product development priorities

📊 Infrastructure, ecosystem, and scalability work

We believe in building in the open — this page is part of that commitment.

Note: Items listed here are not guaranteed release targets or deadlines. Priorities may shift based on technical discoveries, user demand, or ecosystem needs.

For the latest product updates or changelogs, please refer to our Release Notes or Dev Updates on X.

UniSat Website: [https://unisat.io/](https://unisat.io/)

X: [https://x.com/unisat\_wallet](https://x.com/unisat_wallet)

Discord: [http://discord.gg/unisat](http://discord.gg/unisat)

# Production Roadmap in Q4 2024 | UniSat

As we enter the final quarter of 2024, our focus remains on delivering and optimizing our products to provide top-tier infrastructure support for both Bitcoin and Fractal. We are excited to share our upcoming roadmap to encourage proactive and meaningful engagement with the community as we continue our journey together.

_(please note this is a draft version that will be revised periodically as we progress)_

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/production-roadmap-in-q4-2024#roadmap-in-q4-2024)

Roadmap in Q4 2024


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/production-roadmap-in-q4-2024#october-2024)

October 2024

*   **Runes activation on Fractal**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Implement Runes on Fractal (lowercase)
        
    *   Post-activation: Enable SimpleBridge to bridge Bitcoin mainnet Runes onto Fractal, so that they can interact with Runes on Fractal directly
        
    
*   **CAT20 identifying and transferring**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   UniSat Wallet: Enable CAT20 recognition, display and transfers
        
    *   UniSat Explorer: Identify CAT20 assets and transactions
        
    
*   **CAT Market (trustless CAT20 trading)**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Implement a trustless, permissionless Bitcoin script-based on-chain CAT20 trading platform
        
    *   Support for both buy orders and sell orders (more flexible than PSBT), but partial order fulfillment is not supported yet due to script limitations (without OP\_MUL)
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/production-roadmap-in-q4-2024#november-2024)

November 2024

*   **Fractal on-chain voting**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Design and implement OP\_CAT-based locking and voting model
        
    *   Apply transparent proposal submission, discussion and adoption for Fractal
        
    
*   **PizzaSwap major update**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   UniSat Points and FB Rewards for specific Liquidity Providers
        
    *   Simplified operating procedures for PizzaSwap
        
    *   Opening up to all tickers on Fractal.
        
    
*   **brc-20, Runes & CAT20 optimization**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Enhance UniSat indexing infrastructure to achieve faster block parsing with all supporting protocols (target response time: 15-30s)
        
    *   Optimize the responsiveness (balance updating and UTXO retrieving) of UniSat Wallet (target response time: 15-30s)
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/production-roadmap-in-q4-2024#december-2024)

December 2024

*   **zkAtomicSwap - effective atomic swapping**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Implement atomic swap between different chains & different protocols
        
    *   Trustless trading mechanism between Fractal and other ecosystem
        
    
*   **CAT Protocol advanced support**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Advanced support for cat721 and cat-dApps across all UniSat products
        
    *   Further consolidating product-side implementation of the CAT protocol
        
    
*   **PizzaSwap major update**
    
    *   (Engineering complexity: ⭐️⭐️⭐️; Technical innovation: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️; Scheduling certainty: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️)
        
    *   Perform the upgrade of the BRC-20 swap module on Bitcoin mainnet.
        
    *   Build unified and consistent accessing model for both Bitcoin and Fractal for PizzaSwap
        
    

UniSat Team

_Last Update: Oct 21, 2024_

_(please note this is a draft version that will be revised periodically as we progress)_

# Developer Center | UniSat

Welcome to the UniSat Developer Center. This is your gateway to integrating with UniSat’s suite of blockchain data services through our Open API.

Over the past two years, UniSat has grown from supporting a handful of trading platforms to empowering hundreds of teams across the BRC-20 and Ordinals ecosystem. Our daily API request volume has grown from hundreds of thousands to tens of millions. Throughout this period, we have continually enhanced the stability and reliability of our services.

Throughout this journey, our priority has remained the same: delivering fast, stable, and reliable data services.

UniSat is committed to continuously improving service stability by investing in development resources. In our new developer center, we will continue to offer developers a monthly free access quota of 5 calls/second, up to 2,000 calls/day API requests.

[PreviousProduction Roadmap in Q4 2024](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/production-roadmap-in-q4-2024)
[NextUniSat Open API](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/unisat-open-api)

# FAQ | UniSat

*   **When will the previously requested API keys expire?**
    
    *   **A:** Previously issued free API Keys will expire on **August 31st**. You can register and apply for a new API Key in our new [developer center](https://developer.unisat.io/account/login)
        .
        
    

*   **What are the differences in the API interfaces before and after the upgrade? Will the data be automatically upgraded?**
    
    *   **A:** There are no changes to the API interfaces before and after the upgrade. The old API Key will automatically expire on August 31st. Users need to register and apply for a new API Key at [Developer Center](https://developer.unisat.io/plan)
        
    

*   **Is the data structure of the new API interface consistent with the old API interface?**
    
    *   **A:** Yes, the data structure of the new API interface is consistent with the old one.
        
    

*   **What should I do if my API request limit is not sufficient? What if the rate limit is not enough? What if I exceed my plan's limit?**
    
    *   **A:** This situation typically occurs when your current usage exceeds the limits of your monthly API Key plan. However, there's no need to worry. We offer a "**Pay as you go**" plan that allows you to acquire additional requests as needed. Additionally, we provide **Free**, **Specialist**, **Enterprise**, and **Custom API plans** that you can upgrade to according to your needs, usually with immediate effect.
        
    

[PreviousEnable the two-factor authentication](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/enable-the-two-factor-authentication)
[NextDeveloper Service Legal Disclaimer](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/developer-service-legal-disclaimer)

# Plans | UniSat

To provide everyone with convenient and diverse options for purchasing API keys, we offer several plans: **Free**, **Specialist**, **Enterprise**, **Custom**, and **'Pay as you go'**. For details: [unisat.io/plans](https://unisat.io/plans)

*   **Free**: Ideal for conducting research and high-load testing. Obtain a one-time key for your short-term project.
    

✔Rate Limit: 2,000 calls/day

✔Rate Limit: 5 calls/second

*   **Specialist**: Suitable for developers running larger scripts and blockchain startups with a growing user base.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FMSHWsEfWuCl9bGvDAf1N%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6fa7136-d8e2-47d3-b426-b322b0d72f64&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17e54897&sv=2)

*   **Enterprise**: Perfect for wallets, exchanges, and startups in their growth phase.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FCTkBgFgNg8XYhQPrU8bg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee410ce8-a497-40e3-a314-f30f0a9d834e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0cbae6e&sv=2)

*   **Custom**: To inquire about a custom API plan, please feel free to contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
    .
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FID8h4DzOshXlMV38sHGT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D588b6121-9f4e-4dd3-8bb7-0b93a9742169&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d38a134&sv=2)

*   **Pay as you go**: Suitable for temporary high-demand needs with flexible usage.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FBXJGZ21avjcq51SmejKA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab677c6e-dff2-46f4-8f64-1a0c937c1441&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c258ef75&sv=2)

# Enable the two-factor authentication | UniSat

Two-factor authentication (2FA) is an additional security feature that requires users to enter a six-digit verification code when logging into their accounts. This greatly enhances account security and effectively prevents unauthorized access.

For the safety of your account, we recommend setting up Two-factor authentication immediately after registering to provide an extra layer of protection.

**How to link Two-factor authentication？**

1.  Enter UniSat [Developer Center](https://developer.unisat.io/dashboard)
    , click on the avatar on the right side of the page and select '**2FA Setting**' from the dropdown menu.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F8btJoPCiSTK087n6H8rh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4366c70-2bfc-4045-b249-7517ab4efc36&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94a30c4e&sv=2)

1.  Before binding 2FA, you need to confirm your email to ensure the operation is authorized by you. Click '**Send Code**' on the page, input the verification code received in your email, and click '**Submit**' to enter the 2FA binding page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FkDUfs8dgzOEewucbsQKY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2d440d3-e647-4922-8b73-0829fe024cc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e54d663d&sv=2)

1.  Follow the instructions on the page to first download and install an **authentication app**.
    

iOS: Search **Google Authenticator** in the App Store

Android: Search **Google Authenticator** in Google Play or use [this download link](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.google.android.apps.authenticator2)

Then, use the authenticator app to scan the QR code on the page and enter the six-digit verification code in the authentication app.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FMyoW9mYM8f2RxjeJTsyI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5f204bc-a5df-4567-b6a9-9b74e9eb9e7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b29d544a&sv=2)

1.  Now you are done with 2FA! And of course, you can also disable 2FA if needed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FzitBAQCIznqimmviT8wp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D470acec5-fcce-48d4-8cbe-84f2bc6cae68&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2dd81427&sv=2)

[PreviousHow to Acquire a UniSat API Key](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/how-to-acquire-a-unisat-api-key)
[NextFAQ](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/faq)

# UniSat Wallet | UniSat

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet#unisat-wallet-home-for-your-bitcoin-assets)

**UniSat Wallet — Home for Your Bitcoin Assets**

_Easy and safe to trade, inscribe, and manage assets with UniSat_

UniSat Wallet is the first open-source, non-custodial wallet fully supporting innovative standards on Bitcoin. It provides users with a decentralized, self-custody experience alongside a suite of integrated tools, including:

*   UniSat Marketplace
    
*   UniSat Inscribe
    
*   PizzaSwap — the first open-source AMM DEX built natively on Bitcoin and Fractal
    
*   UTXO Management Tool
    
*   DApp Center
    

Together, these services deliver a one-stop, seamless on-chain experience for Bitcoin and Fractal Bitcoin.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet#key-advantages-of-unisat-wallet)

**Key Advantages of UniSat Wallet:**

*   **Non-Custodial Control:** Your private keys, passwords, and seed phrases are never stored by UniSat. Users retain full control of their keys with no personal data collected.
    
*   **100% Open Source:** All code is available on GitHub, ensuring transparency, security, and community-driven development.
    
*   **Encryption & Security:** Private keys are encrypted locally with your password, providing robust protection for your assets.
    
*   **Privacy First:** UniSat does not track personal data. You can import private keys as "imported" accounts for flexible wallet management.
    
*   **All-in-One Bitcoin & Fractal:** UniSat Wallet supports Native SegWit, Taproot, Nested SegWit, and Legacy address types. You can manage BTC, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes in one place, with multi-seed import and batch address derivation. Seamlessly access UniSat Marketplace, Inscribe, PizzaSwap, UniScan and other services, and switch between Bitcoin and Fractal with a single click.
    
*   **Multi-Platform Support:** Available on iOS, Android, and web browsers for convenient, cross-device access.
    

Being a non-custodial wallet means you will be in full control of managing and safeguarding your assets, including your seed phrase, private keys, and wallet password. You are the only one with access, and thus fully accountable for their security. You will need:

*   Back up your recovery phrase or private keys securely. Losing them means losing your assets permanently.
    
*   Set a strong wallet password and keep it safe. UniSat cannot help recover forgotten passwords.
    
*   Only download UniSat Wallet from the [official website](https://unisat.io/download)
     to avoid fraud or phishing.
    
*   Be cautious when clicking links or downloading software from any source.
    

Stay safe and enjoy your journey with UniSat Wallet!

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet#disclaimer)

Disclaimer:

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, and may depreciate in value. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

# Overview of UniSat 2025 Work Priorities | UniSat

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#work-carried-over-from-2024)

Work carried-over from 2024

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#cat721)

**CAT721**

Let’s start with some ongoing work.

Support for CAT721 on Fractal is expected to be delivered in two phases: wallet and browser support will be delivered by January 10th, and CAT721 market support will be delivered around January 20th, with corresponding community events.

\-Updates from Feb. 2025: The CAT721 marketplace development is complete and awaiting launch. Stay tuned.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#pizzaswap)

**PizzaSwap**

There will be three updates in a row:

a. Simplifying user operations through embedding the bridge in the swap. b. Implementing support for Runes and CAT20. c. Introducing support for the stablecoin SUSD from Shell Finance.

These changes will be delivered over different iterations throughout January.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#product-deliverables-for-2025)

Product Deliverables for 2025

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#brc-20-feature-extensions-and-open-source-indexing-service)

**brc-20 Feature Extensions and Open-Source Indexing Service**

Considering the inconsistencies that have existed with brc-20 on the Bitcoin mainnet, we made a few adjustments to significantly simplify and reduce potential rule complexities for brc-20 on Fractal. These include supporting 6-12 character ticker names, lifting the character constraints for fair-mint and self-issuance, using a simplified standard character set, and so on. For more details, see [here](https://docs.fractalbitcoin.io/doc/brc-20-on-fractal)
.

In terms of expanding brc-20 features, we will attempt further improvements in 2025 on Fractal, including:

*   **One-step transfer:** Simplifying the current mint and transfer into a single step.
    
*   **One-to-many transfer:** Enabling a single transfer to multiple users.
    
*   **Airdrop functionality:** Supporting airdrop transactions with up to 2000 recipients in a single transaction.
    
*   **Phased minting:** Enabling fair minting within a specified block range.
    

We believe that enhancing and expanding these features will make brc-20 a more featured protocol.

Regarding implementation, UniSat will focus more on refining and improving its open-source indexing service. While the previously released open-source index service works, it hasn’t been actively maintained. Our improvement objectives include:

*   Simplifying the system architecture of the open-source index, focusing solely on providing brc-20 index services, without the need to maintain flexible architecture supporting multiple protocols.
    
*   Fully integrating UniSat’s high-performance proprietary brc-20 indexing code into the open-source index service, delivering significant advantages over the official Ordinals index service. Specifically, our high-performance indexing service can process hundreds of blocks per second, with full on-chain data processing taking only a few hours, while the Ordinals index processes one block in a few seconds and requires at least two days to process complete on-chain data.
    
*   In the near future, we aim to transition UniSat’s entire product line to use this open-source index implementation and maintain it actively for the developer community.
    

Long-term, we hope to optimize the index service implementation, introduce new features, and create applications to inject new vitality into brc-20, driving the continued development for the protocol.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#unisat-wallet-2.0)

UniSat Wallet 2.0

We will deliver version 2.0 of UniSat Wallet in Q2. The most critical change will be the security model upgrade. Users will be able to choose from different security models and, when needed, use cross-device interactions for higher security. This version will also support more types of hardware wallets, such as Ledger and Trezor, and gradually support more protocols on Bitcoin.

We’ve been taking note of community feedback, highly requested features such as easier inscription management (categorization and search), handling obsoleted inscriptions or large amount of scattered inscriptions, and managing fragmented UTXOs will be delivered across multiple product updates throughout 2025.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#unisat-explorer-2.0)

UniSat Explorer 2.0

In Q4 of 2024, with the launch of Fractal, we launched a comprehensive block explorer for the Fractal network- UniSat Explorer. This explorer is compatible with different protocols and clearly show asset transfers across protocols like Ordinals, brc-20, Runes, and cat20.

In the new year, we will further enhance UniSat Explorer’s capabilities, expanding to Bitcoin mainnet and ensuring product consistency across different networks. For example, users will be able to conveniently query the asset distribution of a Bitcoin address across different networks with one click.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#unisat-marketplace-2.0)

UniSat Marketplace 2.0

This year, we will fully upgrade the PSBT-based P2P transaction model used by our Marketplace. We are gearing up for a major product and brand upgrade of the Marketplace in Q3. Stay tuned for community events around the release.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#collaboration-and-ecosystem-development-plans-for-2025)

Collaboration and Ecosystem Development Plans for 2025

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#bitcoin-fractal-interoperability)

Bitcoin/Fractal Interoperability

In 2025, our main focus for Fractal Bitcoin will be to enhance interoperability between Bitcoin and Fractal, simplifying asset flow between Bitcoin’s mainnet and Fractal. This will allow Fractal to play a more substantial role in supporting Bitcoin as a system and lay better groundwork for using Fractal to expand Bitcoin. Over the long term, we aim to create a more scalable and flexible system for Bitcoin/Fractal.

The launch of DeTrading, a trustless cross-chain platform for atomic swaps that supports Fractal and Bitcoin networks, marks a major milestone in Bitcoin interoperability. This groundbreaking application of atomic swaps is the first successful attempt to bring a truly trustless cross-chain experience for users.

DeTrading’s solution will play significant role in simplifying and promoting interoperability between Fractal Bitcoin and Bitcoin mainnet. The atomic swap protocol can also support multiple asset types including brc-20, runes and even CAt20, and be expanded to other blockchains like Ethereum and Solana, which makes it a highly universal and adaptable approach. This universal approach paves way for fast transaction channels for different types of assets across various networks. UniSat will support the DeTrading team in refining and improving their product and may also explore structural improvements to existing bridge products.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#constructing-a-hyper-indexer)

Constructing a Hyper Indexer

In 2025, SatWorld will start to create a vibrant virtual world, allowing people to create (avatars), explore (vast unknown worlds), harvest (treasures and resources), build (homes and habitats), and organize various forms of interaction. The virtual world will also have autonomous agents that interact with user avatars, offering more possibilities and variety.

UniSat will collaborate closely with SatWorld, using the Bitcoin/Fractal network infrastructure to help bring this vision into reality. We will improve and optimize the existing indexer, provide a more user-friendly interface that allows virtual world creators to quickly access and use images, sounds, texts, artworks, and concepts existing in millions of inscriptions. By turning on-chain inscription data into a shared library and development repository, UniSat’s indexing service will become a powerful hyper-indexer for managing and retrieving on-chain resources.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#did-system-based-on-unified-addresses)

DID System Based on Unified Addresses

One unique feature of Fractal Bitcoin is its shared address format and transaction structure with Bitcoin, this not only allow Bitcoin users to enjoy Fractal’s expanded block space and utility with ease, but also allows us to create build a global identity and reputation system in the Bitcoin system. You may have noticed that UniSat has started creating different Titles that users can claim for unlocking various achievements. With this system, Users will be able to form and leverage a universal identity and reputation based on their activity and achievements across networks.

In the new year, we will gradually begin to build out this system, starting with the following:

*   UniSat titles
    
*   Domains linked to your Bitcoin/Fractal addresses.
    
*   Interactions with different projects in the Bitcoin/Fractal ecosystem.
    
*   Your on-chain voting history in Fractal Vote.
    
*   Your avatars and gear in SatWorld.
    
*   Changes in your Fractal Bitcoin and other asset holdings.
    

This list will expand as the system is developed. You will gradually see the system rolled out on your UniSat personal asset page. We will accumulate a DID system based on on-chain reputation, allowing you to link addresses used in different periods as part of your identity.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#support-for-stablecoins-yields-ai-agents-and-more)

Support for Stablecoins, Yields, AI Agents, and More

We have already done some preliminary work on stablecoins. Some time in 2025, we plan to begin to provide strong support for stablecoins in our products. For Fractal, stablecoins with low fees will become a critical part of transactions, thereby driving the development of more use cases.

In December 2024, UniSat Wallet integrated Babylon's service. We will also engage with more projects that generate yield from holding assets and actively explore native yield models on Fractal Bitcoin.

We have observed that active AI agents are beginning to support Bitcoin, and we will contribute code to support Ordinals, Runes, and Fractal Bitcoin, ensuring that these agents can operate inscriptions and other assets without obstacles.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/overview-of-unisat-2025-work-priorities#conclusion)

Conclusion

This document shares a brief overview of our development plans for 2025. As our work progresses, we will update this plan periodically. In the coming year, we will focus on integrating development and operational resources more effectively, serving Bitcoin users more holistically, and fostering a more open industry atmosphere. We aim to collaborate more actively with different teams and communities, explore innovative ideas, contribute more open-source code, and organize more community activities, creating greater value and opportunities for users and developers.

_(This document will be updated as work progresses, Last Update: 2025-01-05)_

[PreviousUniSat 2025 Q2 Work priorities](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/unisat-2025-q2-work-priorities)
[NextProduction Roadmap in Q4 2024](https://docs.unisat.io/welcome/unisat-work-priorities/production-roadmap-in-q4-2024)

Last updated 4 months ago

# How to Acquire a UniSat API Key | UniSat

Previously, API keys were requested by contacting the UniSat team and applying via email. With the new Developer Center, you will need to register with your email and choose the appropriate plan.

Here are the steps to acquire a UniSat API Key:

1.  Visit [UniSat website](https://unisat.io/)
     and click 'Developer' in the homepage navigation bar. From the dropdown menu, select 'API Pricing' to access the detailed API plans page. Alternatively, you can directly click [here](https://unisat.io/plans)
     to view the API plans.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FnyfTQ18WrhfmnTi8o2Qf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D511ded8c-9a1a-489b-946a-590764c93b5f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17fde198&sv=2)

1.  Choose the plan that suits your needs and click '**Get Started**' under the detailed description of the plan to go to the Developer Center plan acquire page. Or you can click '**Developer Center**' in the yellow box on the page to enter the Developer Center.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKvSlgUIPuOpZ55GgHIk5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33f3b31c-48e4-4978-81b7-fa555d3bef00&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b49347f6&sv=2)

1.  Before acquiring a plan, you need to register a Developer Center account using your email.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FBlkwVnfSxnSD4tZOWYtX%252F20240716-205021.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40744b9b-b4e3-49d0-bb93-9f5905579447&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44e14a5&sv=2)

1.  Once registered, go to the Dashboard page where you will see your API Key, Current API Key Configuration, and your API Request Log. For newly registered accounts, we will continue to offer developers a monthly free access quota of 5 calls/second, up to 2,000 calls/day.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FUAhMoqaGxp2JstQxIrRO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10328495-ef97-44dc-acf9-6bcf40dd08b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90717a9e&sv=2)

Click '**Plan**' in the upper left corner to go to the API Key acquire page.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FPuNcrDvSNVJLKrkwgdVp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df95cc767-1365-418f-9c0b-ecbd683b1033&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7156777c&sv=2)

1.  Choose the plan you need and click the '**Buy**' button under the specific plan to enter the acquire page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FhT0EEePTYKRgREA9WTpC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7c487c7-7aa4-4b50-ae44-eb2f3f309cc5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c3073fc3&sv=2)

1.  Payments are currently accepted via PayPal and BTC. If you choose PayPal, the page will redirect to the PayPal payment page. If you choose BTC, you can pay using a BTC wallet address or your UniSat wallet.
    

Here is an example of a BTC payment method, click '**Pay with BTC**', then select '**Pay with Wallet**'. The page will prompt you to sign; confirm the input and output information carefully, and click 'Sign & Pay' to complete the acquire.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fw1zcL9rjBCnkyjfIEH8X%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1e81f91-f4f7-46bc-9935-a47eafe95956&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=779bf631&sv=2)

1.  After the acquire is complete, you can view your plan acquire record on the **Billing** page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FD7eU8reBYzfB1dTHwEZH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5339f0b8-1ca4-4ef5-9396-0246332a24fc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3519781&sv=2)

[PreviousPlans](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/plans)
[NextEnable the two-factor authentication](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/enable-the-two-factor-authentication)

# Release Notes | UniSat

Welcome to the UniSat Wallet – Release Notes!

Here you’ll find a complete history of updates to the UniSat browser extension wallet — including feature improvements, bug fixes, newly supported protocols, and user experience enhancements.

We created this space to help you stay informed about how UniSat Wallet evolves over time and to give you better insight into the product’s latest developments.

Thank you for your continued support and feedback.

*   Explore our latest products: [https://unisat.io](https://unisat.io/)
    
*   Follow us on X for real-time updates: [https://x.com/unisat\_wallet](https://x.com/unisat_wallet)
    
*   Join our Discord for support & discussions: [http://discord.gg/unisat](http://discord.gg/unisat)

**Features:**

🔸 Multi-Signature Support for Whitelisted SitesFor whitelisted websites, you can now sign multiple transactions with a single click, simplifying batch transactions.

⚠️ _Please note that UniSat Wallet will not verify each transaction individually. We strongly recommend using this feature only on trusted and familiar websites to minimize the risk of potential losses._

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKouVWvcRJhD04Lqh92bV%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c2440ad-ac13-49ea-ba9b-f278cb9c8645&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8f16db4&sv=2)

# Best Practices for Safety | UniSat

By staying informed and following these guidelines, you can significantly reduce the risk of falling victim to scams and malicious activities in the cryptocurrency space. Remember, your wallet’s security is ultimately in your hands, so take the necessary precautions to keep your funds safe.

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#avoid-malicious-websites-and-scammers)

**Avoid malicious websites and scammers**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’d like to make sure you’re aware of common scams and phishing attempts, so you can be ready if you ever encounter them. Most scams use similar tricks, often trying to get your private information to access your cryptocurrency. Stay vigilant!

*   **Beware of Unsolicited Messages** Be cautious about clicking on links received via Discord, Telegram, email, or other social media, especially if they are unsolicited. Scammers often use phishing emails or messages to trick users into visiting malicious websites. If you receive an unexpected communication, verify its legitimacy with UniSat Wallet’s official channels. **UniSat staff will never message you directly.**
    
*   **UniSat & UniSat staff will never ask for your secret recovery phrase or private key.**
    
*   **Double-Check URLs** Always verify the legitimacy of the websites you visit. Scammers often create fake websites that mimic official platforms. Before entering any sensitive information, double-check the URL for spelling mistakes or unusual characters. Official UniSat Wallet websites will always use secure protocols like HTTPS.
    
*   **Verify Announcements** Scammers may create fake announcements that appear to come from official sources. Before taking any action based on an announcement, verify its authenticity by cross-referencing with UniSat Wallet’s official channels.
    
*   **Educate Yourself** Stay informed about common scams and phishing techniques prevalent in the cryptocurrency space. Knowledge is your first line of defense. Familiarize yourself with the typical tactics scammers use, such as fake websites, phishing emails, and fraudulent announcements.
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#official-channels)

Official Channels

Ensuring the safety of your UniSat Wallet is our top priority. Unfortunately, scammers and impersonators are on the rise, attempting to deceive users and compromise their assets. To safeguard your funds, it's crucial to only interact with our verified and official channels.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#verified-organization-on-x-yellow-checkmark)

**Verified Organization on X (Yellow checkmark)**

UniSat has been verified as an organization on X, and you can easily identify us by the yellow checkmark associated with our name. This verification serves as a stamp of authenticity, assuring you that you are engaging with the legitimate UniSat organization.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#exclusive-support-channel-on-discord)

**Exclusive Support Channel on Discord**

When it comes to seeking assistance, the only official channel for customer service is the support ticket system on our Discord server. Beware of individuals reaching out to you through other means, especially DMs or external platforms, claiming to be UniSat support.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#safety-tips)

Safety Tips

You should never share your recovery phrase or private key with anyone. Follow these rules to stay safe:

*   Install the official UniSat Wallet browser extension and avoid installing a fake extension.
    
*   UniSat & UniSat staff will never ask for your secret recovery phrase or private key. UniSat staff will never message you directly first.
    
*   Never enter your private key or secret recovery phrase on any website unless you know what you are doing.
    
*   Avoid interacting with suspicious websites using UniSat Wallet browser extension.
    
*   Keep your UniSat Wallet browser extension up-to-date.
    
*   There is no UniSat Airdrop. Don't trust airdrop or giveaway messages. If you’re unsure you can ask our staff about your concerns in discord or twitter.
    
*   Keep your system security/anti-virus updated so your wallet keys do not get compromised.
    

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#keep-your-secret-recovery-phrase-secure)

Keep your Secret Recovery Phrase secure


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UniSat Wallet is used to sign transactions when interacting with the Bitcoin blockchain, as well as to store your BRC-20s, NFTs, and other kinds of inscriptions. You receive a 12-word Secret Recovery Phrase when you first create your wallet. It provides access to all the addresses within your wallet. You should never share your secret recovery phrase or private key with anyone.

UniSat Wallet does not control any of your personal or private data on servers. Your wallet data is encrypted in your browser and guarded with your UniSat Wallet password.

When you lose password access to your accounts and need to restore them, you can only do that with your Secret Recovery Phrase. So keep your Secret Recovery Phrase safe and secure!

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#protect-yourself-on-discord)

Protect yourself on Discord


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users are increasingly being targeted by scammers and impersonators on Discord. Here's what you can do to increase your safety on Discord. We recommend you adjust the following Discord settings to reduce risks.

*   **Turn off server-specific DMs:** Right-click on a **server icon > Privacy Settings** to allow or disallow direct messages from users of that particular server. Turn it off for large public servers such as UniSat Discord.
    
*   **Turn off DMs:** In user **settings > Privacy & Safety**, you can control who can send you direct messages. Consider turning them off by default for added security.
    
*   **Enable 2-Factor Authentication (2FA):** In **user settings > My Account, s**croll down and set up both an authentication app and SMS authentication. Download your backup codes for 2-FA access in case of emergencies.
    
*   **Verify User Identities:** Right-click a user's profile > Copy ID, verify the ID with the server's staff to confirm the identity. If in doubt, reach out to us via our official channels.
    

By following these tips and staying vigilant, you can protect yourself from scammers and enjoy your time on Discord. Remember, it's always better to be cautious than sorry!

[PreviousUniSat Wallet Safety Guide: Protecting Your Assets](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets)
[NextUniSat Inscribe](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe)

Last updated 1 year ago

# UniSat Marketplace | UniSat

UniSat Marketplace is a decentralized marketplace that makes it easy and secure to trade and manage Bitcoin-native assets, including brc-20, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes. Since launching in 2023, UniSat has become a trusted, open-source tool known for its user-first approach, competitive fees, and seamless integration across the Bitcoin and Fractal network.

Whether you're looking to trade your first brc-20 tickers, Runes, or Alkanes, or securely manage your Bitcoin assets, UniSat Marketplace provides the tools and infrastructure to make it simpler, cheaper, and smoother.

UniSat Marketplace: [https://unisat.io/market](https://unisat.io/market)

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/unisat-marketplace#key-features-of-the-unisat-marketplace)

Key Features of the UniSat Marketplace

*   **Multi-Protocol Asset Support - Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes Assets:** Trade and manage Ordinals, brc-20 tickers, Runes, Alkanes, Names, and Collections—all fully compliant with Bitcoin mainnet standards. No third-party bridges or custodians required.
    
*   **Decentralized & Non-Custodial:** UniSat never stores your mnemonic phrases or private keys. All trades are signed directly via your wallet, giving you full control over your assets.
    
*   **Low & Competitive Fees:** Enjoy just 0.5% service fees for trading brc-20 tickers, Runes, Alkanes, Names, and Collections, ensuring cost-effective market participation. Small orders may even qualify for zero fees—see detailed [fee info](https://docs.unisat.io/unisat-marketplace/unisat-marketplace-fee-rates)
     for more.
    
*   **Seamless Integration:** Compatible with UniSat Wallet, OKX Wallet, Magic Eden Wallet, Xverse, and more and supports switching between Bitcoin and Fractal marketplaces in one click, making transactions and operations more convenient. Deeply integrated with UniSat Wallet, UniScan, Inscribe service, and PizzaSwap, making advanced operations and data access more convenient.
    
*   **Developer-Friendly:** All trading, listing, and indexing logic follows open protocols. With our [public APIs](https://docs.unisat.io/dev/developer-center/unisat-open-api)
    , developers can freely build custom tools or marketplaces without permission.
    
*   **User-Centric Experience:** Clean UI with one-click listing and buying, real-time asset rankings, and automatic UTXO management. Powered by PSBT for enhanced security and flexibility. We continuously improve the experience based on community feedback.
    

UniSat Marketplace is your gateway to exploring Bitcoin-native assets—secure, efficient, and always improving based on community feedback.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/unisat-marketplace#disclaimer)

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, and may depreciate in value. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

# Inscribing brc-20 and Runes in a single transaction | UniSat

UniSat supports inscribing brc-20 and Runes in a single transaction! This means you can inscribe Runes alongside brc-20 in a more cost-efficient way compared to inscribing them separately.

**How is this achieved?**

Whether you are inscribing a BRC-20 ticker or making a regular BTC transfer, any Bitcoin transaction with an OP\_RETURN data size of 16 bytes or more will automatically mint a runes ticker.

In other words, if the fee rate is 1 sat/vB, the minting cost of 1 runes ticker is 16 sats because of the 16 bytes OP\_RETURN data.

**What's new?**

*   Simultaneously inscribe BRC-20 and Runes in one UTXO
    
*   Save on inscribing fees
    
*   Faster & more efficient inscribing
    
*   On both Bitcoin and Fractal mainnet
    

**What are the potential drawbacks?**

If you mint 1000 A brc-20 tickers for instance, you will also generate 1,000 B runes tickers, each associated with a separate UTXO. If you do not consolidate these B tickers later, you will only be able to sell them one by one.

Additionally, since BRC-20 tokens and Runes tokens exist within the same UTXO, some applications may have difficulty distinguishing between them, potentially leading to asset misidentification and loss.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FYUHk6S1umfIJU54Wzkoj%252Fmut.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2efac2c0-b4b2-40a0-ab3e-cad95dc2ce22&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13a665e5&sv=2)

[PreviousHow to Inscribe on UniSat](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat)
[NextAdvanced Features](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/advanced-features)

# Chrome Extension FAQ | UniSat

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/chrome-extension-faq#how-to-update-your-wallet)

**How to update your wallet?**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Usually, the extension will be auto-updated. If your extension didn't update to the latest version, then you may follow the steps below to update it.

1.  Click on the extension icon on the top right of your screen, then click "Manage extensions" menu.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FeDFIda7RCXQrg2ncvLm3%252Fimg_v3_026q_a2918678-741c-45fc-a0f4-dbc36576b3hu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf0edf91-e02f-4064-8526-d82afc3691ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c488c3a&sv=2)

1.  Switch on to Developer mode, then click the "Update" button
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FV5jZbC3rwjPBgitQV9qw%252Fimg_v3_026q_5231b2ca-3a51-471b-9c38-078f133b53hu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5612902d-caf4-4da4-a42c-55e93ad0b7d9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a2b9ff1&sv=2)

1.  Then your wallet will be updated to the latest version.
    

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/chrome-extension-faq#how-to-load-the-chrome-extension-wallet-into-your-chrome-from-manually)

How to load the Chrome extension wallet into your Chrome from manually


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The extension could be temporarily installed this way:

1.  Download the '[**unisat-chrome-xxx.zip**](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/extension/releases/latest)
    ' file, unzip it to an isolated folder. ![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FtHf0ep2PdhLcbJ0IEhoj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D343f807f-c65b-4138-8b94-b3a65153e182&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=56f99ebe&sv=2)
    
2.  Open Google Chrome and enter "**chrome://extensions/**" into address bar ("More Tools | Extensions" from menu) to open the extension page, find the switch "**Developer mode**" in the upper right corner and turn it on. ![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fxiq4m6HasR5Hx1Mid5KP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09c7df65-3d13-4f70-8571-77516cebd29c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9dceae45&sv=2)
    
3.  Click "**Load unpacked**" button and browse to the unzipped folder. ![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FQfUVYFBDZR0m7JO3GpEg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D160fc102-43cf-4d31-a3ea-d1f89f1ccd96&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59a040f8&sv=2)
    

*   By doing this, you can experience the new version in advance or install the plugin in cases where you cannot access the Google Chrome Web Store.
    
*   However, please note that versions installed in this way won't receive automatic updates and won't share data with versions downloaded from the Chrome Web Store.
    
*   Make sure you have only one Unisat Wallet plugin installed in the same browser to avoid conflicts.

# UniSat Wallet Safety Guide: Protecting Your Assets | UniSat

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#understanding-the-risks)

Understanding the Risks

Browser extension wallets have become an essential tool for managing digital assets, but they come with inherent security risks that every user should understand:

**Browser Sandbox Limitations**

The browser's built-in sandbox mechanism, while important, serves as a single line of defense. This makes it a potential target for sophisticated attacks, as breaking this one mechanism could compromise the entire system.

**Weak Extension Isolation**

Extensions within the same browser environment have limited isolation from each other. This creates a "weakest link" scenario - if one extension is compromised, it could potentially affect all others in the same browser environment, including your wallet extension.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#essential-safety-practices)

Essential Safety Practices

To protect your digital assets when using extension wallets, consider implementing these security measures:

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-1.-browser-account-separation)

1\. Browser Account Separation

Create a dedicated browser profile for your wallet extensions. This profile should:

*   Install only essential wallet extensions
    
*   Be kept separate from your daily browsing profile
    
*   Use a separate account for each wallet extension where possible
    

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-2.-restricted-browsing)

2\. Restricted Browsing

When using a browser with wallet extensions:

*   Only visit verified, trusted websites
    
*   Avoid general web browsing
    
*   Stay away from unfamiliar or suspicious links
    
*   Always verify website URLs carefully
    

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-3.-duo-browser-strategy)

3\. Duo-Browser Strategy

For maximum security:

*   Use one browser exclusively for wallet extensions and cryptocurrency transactions
    
*   Use a different browser for general web browsing
    
*   Keep your crypto-dedicated browser clean and minimal
    

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-4.-hardware-wallet-integration)

4\. Hardware Wallet Integration

Consider using a hardware wallet as your primary security measure:

*   Hardware wallets provide the highest level of security
    
*   Use them in conjunction with extension wallets for enhanced protection
    
*   Keep critical assets in hardware wallets while using extension wallets for smaller, frequent transactions
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#about-unisat-wallet)

About UniSat Wallet

UniSat is a non-custodial, open-source browser extension wallet. This means:

*   We never store or have access to your private keys
    
*   You have complete control over your assets
    
*   All code is open-source and verifiable
    
*   Your funds remain solely in your possession
    

While we maintain the highest security standards possible for an extension wallet, we believe in complete transparency about the inherent risks of browser-based wallets and empowering users with security best practices.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#looking-forward)

Looking Forward

We understand that in today's increasingly complex digital environment, wallet security cannot rely solely on traditional browser protection mechanisms. At UniSat Wallet, we're committed to strengthening our extension's security mechanisms to provide users with a safer experience, this is a key item on our 2025 Roadmap.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#final-recommendations)

Final Recommendations

1.  Regular Security Audits
    

*   Review your installed extensions regularly
    
*   Remove unused or suspicious extensions
    
*   Keep your wallet extension updated to the latest version
    

1.  Best Practices
    

*   Always backup your seed phrases securely
    
*   Enable all available security features
    
*   Use strong, unique passwords for your browser profiles
    
*   Enable two-factor authentication whenever possible
    

Remember: Security in the digital asset space requires constant vigilance. While convenience is important, never compromise security for ease of use.

[PreviousChrome Extension FAQ](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/chrome-extension-faq)
[NextBest Practices for Safety](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety)

**🎨 Delegate: Save big when mass-minting copies!**

Delegate lets you create copies of an inscription easily by nominating a “delegate” (the original copy). Imagine repeat-minting 1000 images in one go!

It save storing content for each inscription and therefore saves fees too! Requests for the content of an inscription with a delegate will instead return the content, content type and content encoding of the delegate.

ICYDK, UniSat OG pass collection was minted with this method! This helped us save big on fees.

Learn more about Delegate : [https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/delegate.html](https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/delegate.html)

*   Great for NFT and game assets creators.

With the Pointer option, you can choose exactly which utxo or sats (satoshi) your inscription gets minted on, like rare sats!

*   This gives builders more control over sats

# Understanding UTXO | UniSat

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#what-is-utxo)

What is UTXO?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UTXO (Unspent Transaction Output) is a fundamental concept in Bitcoin and many other blockchain networks. It represents the unspent outputs of previous transactions that can be used as inputs for new transactions. Essentially, a UTXO is like a physical cash bill—you can only spend it as a whole, and any leftover balance is returned as change in a new bill (UTXO). This model differs from Ethereum’s account-based model, where balances are updated directly. Unlike traditional bank accounts, where money is summed up into a single balance, Bitcoin transactions require selecting specific UTXOs for spending, similar to using exact change when making a purchase.

* * *

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#how-utxo-increases-and-decreases)

How UTXO Increases and Decreases?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UTXOs increase when a Bitcoin transaction generates new outputs. For example, if Alice sends 0.5 BTC to Bob, a new UTXO worth 0.5 BTC is created in Bob’s wallet. If Alice had 1 BTC before the transaction, the remaining balance of 0.5 BTC minus any transaction fees is returned to her as a new UTXO.

Conversely, UTXOs decrease when they are used as inputs in transactions. When Bob later sends 0.2 BTC to Charlie, his 0.5 BTC UTXO is consumed, and two new UTXOs are created: one for Charlie (0.2 BTC) and one as change returned to Bob (0.3 BTC minus fees). This mechanism ensures that all Bitcoin transactions follow a clear and traceable path.

Any Bitcoin transaction, including sending BTC, minting or transferring inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers, may increase or decrease UTXOs.

* * *

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#unlocking-utxos-benefits-and-risks)

Unlocking UTXOs: Benefits and Risks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Many users inscribe inscriptions or mint Runes and BRC-20 tickers, resulting in small UTXOs that hold these assets containing only 546 sats. To prevent these asset-containing UTXOs from being spent as miner fees and leading to asset loss, Bitcoin wallets tend to lock them by default, making them unspendable. You may have some 'useless assets' in UTXOs like BRC-20 mint inscriptions, transfer inscriptions.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#benefits-of-unlocking-utxos)

Benefits of Unlocking UTXOs:

**Immediate Usability**: Once unlocked, these UTXOs can be directly used as Bitcoin for transactions.**User Control**: UniSat wallet allows users to decide whether to unlock specific UTXOs. Before confirming a transaction, the wallet will display whether a UTXO contains a particular asset, enabling informed decision-making.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#risks-of-unlocking-utxos)

Risks of Unlocking UTXOs:

**Potential Asset Loss**: If an unlocked UTXO contains inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers you wanna hold, it will be spent as regular Bitcoin. This means that if such a UTXO is included in a transaction, the associated assets may be irreversibly sent to the recipient, leading to loss.

* * *

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#splitting-and-merging-utxos)

Splitting and Merging UTXOs:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#when-to-use-them)

When to Use Them?

Splitting UTXOs involves breaking a large UTXO into smaller ones. This is useful in scenarios such as:

**Enabling Multiple Transactions**: Having smaller UTXOs allows users to initiate multiple transactions simultaneously. This is especially useful for minting inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers, where users may need to broadcast multiple minting transactions quickly without being stopped by pending(unconfirmed) UTXOs.

**Preventing Asset Mixing**: Users who manage both Bitcoin and Bitcoin ecosystem assets (inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers) may split UTXOs to keep asset-containing UTXOs separate from pure Bitcoin UTXOs.

Merging UTXOs is the opposite process, where multiple smaller UTXOs are combined into a single larger one. This is beneficial when:

**Reducing Transaction Fees**: Users who have accumulated many small UTXOs (e.g., 546 sats, 1000 sats) from minting inscriptions may find that transactions become costly due to the high number of inputs. Merging these UTXOs reduces the input count and lowers transaction fees.

**Wallet Management**: Consolidating UTXOs into fewer, larger UTXOs makes managing funds more efficient, especially for users frequently engaging with Bitcoin-based assets. You can merge many small UTXOs only containing 546 sats or 1000 sats into a larger one.

[PreviousUTXO Management](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management)
[NextHow to reclaim BTC/FB trapped in useless inscription UTXOs](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-reclaim-btc-fb-trapped-in-useless-inscription-utxos)

# UniSat Inscribe | UniSat

UniSat Inscribe is a powerful and user-friendly tool designed for creators, developers, and users to seamlessly inscribe. Supporting both Bitcoin and Fractal networks, UniSat offers full compatibility with multiple inscription standards—including Ordinals (brc-20, text, files, names) and Runes (mint and etch)—for a secure and efficient inscription experience.

🔗 [https://unisat.io/inscribe](https://unisat.io/inscribe)

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#why-use-unisat-inscribe)

Why Use UniSat Inscribe?

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-1.-multi-protocol-support-and-diverse-inscribing-types)

1\. Multi-Protocol Support & Diverse Inscribing Types

**On Bitcoin:**

*   Ordinals Mint & Deploy
    
    *   4-byte brc-20 tickers & 5-byte brc-20 tickers
        
    *   Inscribing types
        
        *   **brc-20**
            
        *   **Text**
            
        *   **Files:** Including `.jpg`, `.webp`, `.png`, `.gif`, `.txt`, `.mp3`, `.mp4 (H.264)`, and more.
            
        *   **Names:** Including `sats`, `xbt`, `unisat`, `ord`, `btc`, `gm`, and `uniworlds`
            
        
    
*   Runes Mint & Etch
    

**On Fractal:**

*   Ordinals Mint & Deploy
    
    *   **brc-20**
        
    *   **Text**
        
    *   **Files:** Including `.jpg`, `.webp`, `.png`, `.gif`, `.txt`, `.mp3`, `.mp4 (H264)`, and more.
        
    *   **Names:** Including `fb`
        
    
*   Runes Mint & Etch
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-2.-batch-minting-capabilities)

2\. Batch Minting Capabilities

UniSat allows up to **1,000 brc-20 or Runes items** in a single batch order on Bitcoin. Users can:

*   Use **Repeat mint** up to 1,000 items in a single transaction.
    
*   Upload multiple files or datasets for batch inscription.
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-3.-file-size-and-format-limits)

3\. File Size & Format Limits

*   **Maximum file size (per file):** 365 KB
    
*   **Total size per batch:** 750 KB UniSat automatically validates file types and size. Unsupported formats or oversized files will be rejected.
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-4.-affordable-and-transparent-fees)

4\. **Affordable & Transparent Fees**

UniSat Inscribe offers service fees below market average, helping you reduce inscription costs more effectively. Before isncribing, you can customize your network fee, and the system will provide real-time cost estimates based on your selected rate—ensuring both priority and cost-efficiency in your transactions.

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-5.-advanced-inscription-features)

5\. Advanced Inscription Features

UniSat Inscribe supports advanced minting capabilities:

*   Parent/Child Provenance
    
*   Delegate
    
*   Metadata
    
*   Reinscription
    
*   Combined brc-20 and Runes minting in a single transaction
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-6.-seamless-integration)

6\. Seamless Integration

UniSat Inscribe is tightly integrated with the UniSat services:

*   UniSat Wallet
    
*   UniScan
    
*   UniSat Marketplace
    
*   PizzaSwap
    

Combined, these tools offer a streamlined, end-to-end experience for managing, tracking, and trading inscriptions.

UniSat Inscribe is built to provide a robust and continuously improving isncribing service, offering diverse and customizable minting options—while ensuring a secure and efficient experience across both Bitcoin and Fractal.

# How to merge Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB? | UniSat

The Merge function in the UniSat UTXO Management Tool helps consolidate multiple fragmented UTXOs into a single UTXO, making your asset structure more efficient and easier to manage.

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-merge-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#supported-merge-scenarios)

**Supported Merge Scenarios**

*   **Alkanes**: Custom merge up to 500 Alkanes UTXOs UTXOinto a single .
    
*   **Runes**: Custom merge up to 500 Runes UTXOs into a single UTXO.
    
*   **BTC**(on Bitcoin) / **FB** (on Fractal): Merge up to 500 UTXOs into a single UTXO.
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-merge-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#how-to-merge-your-utxos)

**How to Merge** Your **UTXOs？**

In this guide, we will use Merging Alkanes UTXOs as an example. The merging process for Runes, Alkanes, and BTC/FB is generally similar, with slight differences based on the asset type. Please refer to the specific merge interface for each asset.

**Visit:** [https://unisat.io/utxo](https://unisat.io/utxo)

**⚠ Always double-check all details before confirming.**

**⚠ Only UTXOs of the same asset type and same asset name can be merged.**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F4izp44d6PTgsrElSh2KO%252Fmerge.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54b1616c-e756-462e-abcc-7afa6dd43706&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e761c98e&sv=2)

# UniSat Drops | UniSat

*   **What is UniSat Drops**
    

Drops is our way to show our love for Art on Bitcoin and to say thank you to the community by awarding benefits based on Proof of Contribution.

Drops creatively uses UniSat Titles as eligibility to participate so creators can get maximum exposure to UniSat Title holders who represent the most active and significant contributors to the bitcoin community!

*   **What is UniSat Title**
    

UniSat Titles are your personal collection of digital medals that celebrate your journey in the UniSat community!

Each title marks a moment in time when you’ve helped make Bitcoin grow and thrive. As you collect more Titles, you'll unlock exciting new ways to earn benefits from UniSat and our partners, starting with UniSat Drops. More titles will be released as our community continues to grow.

*   **What is Drops Pool**
    

Each Drops Pool contains rewards provided by a Bitcoin project, and has a designated start and end time. Eligible community members can enter the raffle to win rewards for each Pool.

*   **How are winners selected?**
    

Winners are determined by a completely randomized algorithm after the raffle period ends.

The last 6 characters of the latest block hash on Bitcoin or Fractal network is used as a random seed to determine the winner addresses fairly. If the project is issued on Bitcoin, the latest block hash on Bitcoin one hour after the raffle ended will be used.

*   **Which networks do UniSat Drops Support?**
    

UniSat Drops currently supports Bitcoin and Fractal networks.

*   **How to participate in Drops.**
    

1.  Visit [https://unisat.io/drops](https://unisat.io/drops)
     or navigate to the Drops Icon on the top right hand.
    
2.  Check eligibility: Connect your wallet to check eligibility to participate in pools
    
3.  Join raffle: Click Join Raffle.
    
4.  Raffle results: Raffle results will be announced after raffle ends. You will receive a pop-up notification if you are a winner. You can view all winner addresses under ‘Raffle Winners.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fj1s8fDoWrPQQSQAHjVC0%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6960a5b-96aa-4948-a2fa-3aa834afd2ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eaeb03e5&sv=2)

*   **How to submit your project for Drops**
    

You may reach out to us via this form for collaboration.

[https://docs.google.com/forms/d/11jS\_Z3BJ5S7bLemqf12O6PLmTl9ds-OwAAcJuWEz1lQ/edit](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/11jS_Z3BJ5S7bLemqf12O6PLmTl9ds-OwAAcJuWEz1lQ/edit)

[PreviousFAQ](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/faq)
[NextUniSat Points](https://docs.unisat.io/community/unisat-points)

Last updated 1 month ago

---

# How to batch send Ordinals / Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB? | UniSat

The Batch Send function in UniSat UTXO Management Tool helps you efficiently transfer assets to one or multiple addresses, saving time and optimizing UTXO usage.

UniSat UTXO Management Tool: [https://unisat.io/utxo](https://unisat.io/utxo)

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#supported-batch-send-scenarios)

**Supported Batch Send Scenarios**

*   **Alkanes:** Batch send Alkanes UTXOs to multiple addresses with customizable amounts.
    
*   **Ordinals: Batch send** up to 500 inscriptions/collections/name/ brc-20 transfer UTXOs to a designated address, save time and fees.
    
*   **Runes: Batch send** different amounts of Runes to different addresses.
    
*   **BTC(on Bitcoin)/FB(on Fractal): Batch send** up to 500 UTXOs to a single address or up to 1000 different addresses.
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#how-to-batch-send-your-utxos)

How to Batch Send Your UTXOs?

In this guide, we will use Batch Send for Runes as an example. The overall process for Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes, and BTC/FB is similar, with slight differences depending on the asset type. Please refer to the specific batch send interface for each asset.

**⚠️ Note:** _**To avoid sending assets as ordinary BTC, please use the batch send feature within the corresponding protocol-specific page (Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes, BTC/ FB(on Fractal) Tab), don't use batch send under the "All UTXOs" tab.**_

1️⃣ Access the UTXO Management Tool

Visit: [https://unisat.io/utxo](https://unisat.io/utxo)

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-2-select-the-runes-tab)

2️⃣ Select the "Runes" Tab

Switch to the Runes section to manage your Runes UTXOs.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-3-choose-send)

3️⃣ Choose "Send"

Select Runes UTXO and click **Send** button to start the process.

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-4-enter-receiving-addresses-and-amounts)

4️⃣ Enter Receiving Addresses and Amounts

*   Input different addresses and the amount of Runes to send to each address.
    
*   **Double-check all details before confirming.**
    

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-5-confirm-the-transaction)

5️⃣ Confirm the Transaction

Submit the batch send and wait for the transaction to be broadcast to the network.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FTvFzz5M5wQpDBGC0lPki%252Fbatch%2520send.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26ab445d-6b67-46bd-9b52-705743e96961&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58205e54&sv=2)

[PreviousHow to split Ordinals / Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB?](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-split-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb)
[NextHow to merge Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB?](https://docs.unisat.io/utxo-management/how-to-merge-runes-alkanes-btc-fb)

Last updated 18 days ago
