# How to use the Simple Bridge | UniSat

We’re excited to announce that Simple Bridge is live on the Fractal Bitcoin Mainnet! With Simple Bridge, you can securely and efficiently connect assets from different protocols to PizzaSwap and enjoy seamless cross-chain transfers.

Start using it here: [https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge](https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#understand-simple-bridge-rules)

**Understand Simple Bridge Rules**

Before you begin, make sure to familiarize yourself with the Simple Bridge rules.

**Supported Assets:**

*   sBTC, sORDI, sSATS, sQUAQ, sOSHI, sPEPE, sTRAC, sMEME, sRATS, sPIZZA
    
*   All bridged assets carry the **s-** prefix, indicating their status as cross-chain assets transferred via Simple Bridge.
    

**Bridge Fees:**

*   Deposit Fee: 0.00003 BTC
    
*   Withdrawal Fee: 0.25 FB
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#setting-up-your-fractal-bitcoin-wallet)

**Setting Up Your Fractal Bitcoin Wallet**

*   Open the UniSat Wallet extension. You can download it by clicking [here](https://fractal.unisat.io/download)
    .
    

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#using-simple-bridge)

**Using Simple Bridge**

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#step-1-access-the-simple-bridge-page)

**Step 1: Access the Simple Bridge Page**

*   Go to Simple Bridge Page [https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge](https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge)
     and click "Connect" in the top-right corner to sign in with your wallet.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FftcpkZrNsBq45Or00Gtq%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03f341bf-c55d-4dcb-9485-6268f5815ee9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0c0cb5a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#step-2-bridge-btc-or-inscribe-transfer-for-brc-20)

Step 2: Bridge BTC or Inscribe Transfer for brc-20

*   For BTC: Select BTC and simply input the amount you wish to bridge in the "You Pay" section.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fq9vn8pCBvaowMWQK3J3e%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D825addfa-0f34-4227-8c39-13d52294f04b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a934e1bd&sv=2)

*   For brc-20: First, you need to perform an Inscribe Transfer. Select the ticker you want to bridge from the dropdown menu next to the ticker name, then choose a transfer to bridge.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fpb4NVqoMXFh7MR4TyQpi%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7af0ce00-4db2-463a-9089-57280c9d7bcc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81fa9f6c&sv=2)

If you haven't completed an Inscribe Transfer yet, follow the steps below:

*   In the "You Pay" section, select the ticker you wish to bridge and click + to start the Inscribe Transfer.
    
*   In the pop-up signature window, enter the Amount, Output Value, and Fee Rate. After verifying the information is correct, click "Next."
    
*   Confirm the signature details, and click "Next" again.
    
*   Double-check the inputs and outputs in the signature window. Once everything is correct, click "Sign & Pay" to complete the Inscribe Transfer.
    
*   After inscribe transfer, you need to patiently wait for 3 block confirmations.
    
*   Make sure the amount for the Inscribe Transfer is not less than the minimum value specified on the interface.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F0MvwlSda4Z2H3UMX51kc%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2459fc01-22ab-4d5b-ae3d-d78fdd6af568&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e6463e0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F615rmHnsy10tUxkMwol4%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20b3f69e-a79c-4614-94c4-f5af6e7ae18c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14371a8f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#step-3-bridge-operation)

**Step 3: Bridge Operation**

1.  In the Simple Bridge page, select the asset you want to bridge and input the amount in the You Pay field.
    
2.  The system will automatically calculate and display the amount you will receive in the You Receive field. Verify the Receiving Address and Fee. If everything is correct, click Deposit.
    
3.  In the signature window, confirm the inputs and outputs, then click Sign to complete the operation.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F9TrEoK7zwdAMwA1ZPU4d%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dacb7676b-bb24-42d3-ab2a-9e44ec1a8366&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14949298&sv=2)

**Step 4: View Bridge Details**

*   After signing, you'll be taken to the Bridge Details page. The system will automatically complete the bridge operation.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F7j3mOT12dWCch4PEx1R2%252FSim.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D433549fa-37dc-459e-9ccf-867ef7b433de&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5e6efa7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#withdraw-from-simple-bridge)

Withdraw from Simple Bridge

The operations for withdrawing and depositing through the bridge are the same.

First, click the 🔁 icon on the page to switch to withdraw mode.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FExgdZPRwUm1vwKqZW945%252F102.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c285ed2-7014-493f-8828-4929aff6495f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10aeeb82&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#step-1-inscribe-transfer)

**Step 1: Inscribe Transfer**

*   First, you need to perform an Inscribe Transfer. Select the ticker you want to withdraw from the dropdown menu next to the ticker name, then choose a transfer to withdraw.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F52jjg0NBXHZqQ8UFnWn7%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c366651-d486-4be5-bf5f-f39f1c838ff2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2abf4c31&sv=2)

*   If you haven't completed an Inscribe Transfer yet, follow the steps below:In the "You Pay" section, select the ticker you wish to withdraw and click + to perform the Inscribe Transfer.
    
*   In the pop-up signature window, enter the Amount, Output Value, and Fee Rate. After verifying the information is correct, click "Next."
    
*   Confirm the signature details, and click "Next" again.
    
*   Double-check the inputs and outputs in the signature window. Once everything is correct, click "Sign & Pay" to complete the Inscribe Transfer.
    
*   After inscribe transfer, you need to patiently wait for 3 block confirmations.
    
*   Make sure the amount for the Inscribe Transfer is not less than the minimum value specified on the interface.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FqVjG55xe9CFpwqqhe76x%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ba31a33-8e01-49ae-84ae-176eb3a03edd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=647c1558&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FUzA3Oe7fCE0H2ERujM21%252F101.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De10f924f-fb1e-4236-8cdf-3d061ed8a2bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c5719de6&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#step-2-withdraw-operation)

Step 2: Withdraw Operation

1.  In the "You Pay" section, select the ticker you want to withdraw, and click the amount you previously Inscribe Transferred.
    
2.  The system will auto-fill the "You Receive" field with the corresponding amount. Double-check the Receiving Address and Fee. Once confirmed, click "Withdraw."
    
3.  In the signature window, confirm the inputs and outputs, then click "Sign" to complete the process.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FCE8kRnZDh6HEHbY6neLP%252F107.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0762fc8f-1622-4ce7-826d-a82fa7148460&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75643c58&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#step-3-view-withdraw-details)

**Step 3: View Withdraw Details**

*   After signing, you'll be redirected to the Withdraw Bridge Details page. The system will automatically complete the bridge operation.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fwaoy5KB6S0FhoZimN85x%252F109.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df908bd00-c3c8-4a4a-81ad-957978d1c381&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=345d962c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/deprecated/simple-bridge/how-to-use-the-simple-bridge#view-bridge-history)

View Bridge History

You can view your Bridge Deposit and Withdraw history anytime by visiting the Bridge History page: [https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge/history](https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge/history)
.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FGt6xVCnKoLvSztuFuEGK%252F111.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c8c8047-4de1-47ec-b19d-748da24240f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c4698dc&sv=2)

# brc-20 Swap and PizzaSwap Development | UniSat

Before introducing PizzaSwap, it’s essential to understand its roots in brc-20 Swap on Bitcoin Mainnet. As a cornerstone of UniSat’s efforts to push the adoption of brc-20 protocol, we developed the brc-20 Swap alpha on Bitcoin mainnet in November 2023.

Even though the swap on Bitcoin was not able to fully open due to circumstances beyond our control, we’re not giving up. What we learnt from the process paved the way for PizzaSwap- a mirror of the brc-20 swap module on Bitcoin deployed on Fractal Bitcoin- an extension of Bitcoin that is immensely similar to Bitcoin itself.

We’re committed to continuously enhancing the PizzaSwap experience for our users, keeping it secure, efficient, and user-friendly. This timeline traces the journey of brc-20 Swap and PizzaSwap, culminating in our vision for 2025.

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#brc-20-swap-on-bitcoin-mainnet)

brc-20 Swap on Bitcoin Main**net** 🔗


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **2023: Pioneering brc-20 Swap**
    
    *   UniSat launched brc-20 Swap on Bitcoin Mainnet in 2023 after extensive testing throughout 2022-2023.
        
    *   Significant effort and innovation went into ensuring this product functioned correctly on Bitcoin’s mainnet, laying the groundwork for decentralized swaps.
        
    *   More details about brc-20 swap mechanism: [Link](https://docs.unisat.io/knowledge-base/brc20-swap-introduction)
        
    
*   **2024: Standardizing with L1F**
    
    *   Throughout 2024, we worked closely with L1F to integrate brc-20 Swap into the brc-20 standard upgrade. Due to the need for cross-team coordination, the process took longer than expected, but we remained committed to ensuring a smooth and secure implementation.
        
    
*   **2025: Upcoming major protocol upgrades**
    
    *   We continue to work closely with all stakeholders to push forward the brc-20 update, which will introduce three key modules:
        
        *   Single-step TRANSFER
            
        *   Programmable Module
            
        *   Swap Module
            
        
        Learn more: [link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1892537813541007660)
        
    

* * *

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#pizzaswap-on-fractal-bitcoin)

PizzaSwap on Fractal Bitcoin 🍕


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#id-2024-launch-and-evolution)

2024: Launch and Evolution 🚀

PizzaSwap, the first dual-network brc-20 DEX for Bitcoin and Fractal, officially launched on Fractal on September 30, 2024. This swap product, identical in functionality to the mainnet swap module, is the first DEX to be built on both Bitcoin and Fractal.

The launch of PizzaSwap on Fractal is also helping to further drive the development of Swap on the Bitcoin mainnet.

**Key Features**:

*   Swap assets directly, no intermediaries
    
*   Provide liquidity and earn rewards
    
*   Track past transactions in a simple interface
    

Learn more about the **PizzaSwap mechanism**: [Link](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-services/pizzaswap-fractal-swap-service)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#detailed-pizzaswap-timeline)

**Detailed PizzaSwap Timeline** 📅

*   **September 2, 2024**: **Public Testing**
    
    *   Public testing of **PizzaSwap on Fractal Testnet** began to ensure stability and security for the mainnet launch.
        
    *   [Tweet Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1830441537605710242)
        
    
*   **September 30, 2024: Official Launch**
    
    **PizzaSwap officially launched** on Fractal Bitcoin, allowing users to seamlessly swap brc-20 assets on Fractal with ease.
    
    *   First DEX built concurrently on Bitcoin and Fractal, supporting all asset types.
        
    *   Features: Direct swaps, liquidity provision with rewards, and a user-friendly transaction interface.
        
    *   [Tweet Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1840693108255969786)
         | [Docs](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-services/pizzaswap-fractal-swap-service)
        
    
*   **October 2, 2024**: Introduced **Simple Bridge** and **Green Channel**.
    
    *   Simple Bridge enabled smooth asset bridging between Bitcoin and Fractal.
        
    *   Green Channel allowed brc-20 Swap assets from Bitcoin Mainnet to transfer to PizzaSwap.
        
    *   [Tweet Link (Simple Bridge)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1841331216504729955)
        
    *   [Tweet Link (Green Channel)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1841331220841656789)
        
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#ui-and-products-optimizations-and-updates-september-december-2024)

UI & Products Optimizations and Updates **(September - December 2024)** 🔧

From **September 30** to **October 2024**, we’ve continuously worked on improving PizzaSwap’s UI, trading experience, and other features:

*   New Features:
    
    *   Enhanced pool statistics, including TVL & Volume -> [Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1844755657146486793)
        
    *   Optimized asset bridging and deposit process -> [link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1842038490965672099)
        
    *   Enabled withdrawals through partner collaborations -> [Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1847457673106903438)
        
    *   Introduced FB (Fractal Bitcoin) for swap operations and gas fee payments -> [Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1844755267915067466)
        
    *   More details: [Link](https://unisat-wallet.medium.com/2024-10-pizzaswap-unisats-first-open-production-experiment-2c810cd98e7c)
        
    
*   **November 2024**: Opened PizzaSwap to all brc-20 tickers on Fractal, allowing any trading pair creation.
    
    *   [Tweet Link (Support all brc-20 tickers)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1854146491750961416)
        
    
*   **December 2024**: Improved real-time LP earnings display for staking and trading fees.
    
    *   [Tweet Link (Visualization)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1867479699984896143)
        
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#lpfest-on-fractal-november-2024-december-2024)

**LPfest on Fractal (November 2024 - December 2024) 💥**

LPfest is a long-term initiative primarily focused on bringing rewards to liquidity providers.

*   **November 2024**: **LPfest Epoch 1 launched.**
    
    *   LPfest Epoch 1: Introduced sFB <> sBTC, sFB <> sSATS, sFB <> Glizzy pairs with 6,000 FB rewards.
        
    *   [Tweet Link (LPfest Epoch 1)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1854145711635644697)
        
    
*   **December 2024**: Launched **LPfest Epoch 2** and enhanced LP earnings visualization.
    
    *   Epoch 2: Added 5 pairs (sBTC <> sFB, sSATS <> sFB, etc.) with 10,000 FB rewards.
        
    *   Improved real-time LP earnings display for staking and trading fees.
        
    *   [Tweet Link (Epoch 2)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1866033030500135064)
        
    
*   April 2025: LPfest Epoch 3 launched.
    
    *   Introduced 5 trading pair with 10,000 FB in rewards
        
    *   [Tweet Link(Epoch 3)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1913146188809015337)
        
    
*   May 2025: LPfest Epoch 3.1 live with 2 trading pairs with 2,000 FB in rewards.
    
    *   [Tweet Link(Epoch 3.1)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1917527929661317431)
        
    

[](https://docs.unisat.io/technical/brc-20-swap-and-pizzaswap-development#pizzaswap-in-2025)

**PizzaSwap in 2025**🌟


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **January 2025: Testing PizzaSwap 1.1**
    
    The first test version of PizzaSwap 1.1 was launched and tested with a small group of users. We gathered valuable user feedback and conducted research to further improve the product.
    
*   **February 2025**: **PizzaSwap 1.1 launched**
    
    *   Integrated bridge + deposit in one step
        
    *   Dramatically reduced deposit and withdrawal waiting time
        
    *   Zero service fee for deposit
        
    *   [Tweet Post](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1895293661853929664)
        
    
*   **March 10, 2025: Community Vote** - Which Service Fee Level Do You Support for PizzaSwap?
    
    *   Based on extensive community feedback, we have a vote on PizzaSwap’s service fee—let the community decide.
        
    *   [Tweet Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1898672128633004465)
        
    
*   **March 21, 2025: Introduced SUSD•SUSD•SUSD (runes)**
    
    *   SUSD•SUSD•SUSD, an over-collateralized synthetic stablecoin on Bitcoin developed by Shell Finance based on the Runes Protocol.
        
    *   [Tweet Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1903008977820193057)
        
    
*   **April - May 2025, PizzaSwap LPfest Epoch 3 & 3.1 launched**
    
    *   [Tweet Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1913146188809015337)
         [Tweet Link(3.1)](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1917527929661317431)
        
    
*   **April 13: PizzaSwap NEW domain:** [**https://pizzaswap.io/**](https://pizzaswap.io/)
     **& Multilingual support**
    
    *   **NEW domain:** [**https://pizzaswap.io/**](https://pizzaswap.io/)
        
    *   NEW languages - English, French, Spanish, Russian, Japanese, Traditional Chinese
        
    
*   **May 3: PizzaSwap’s Address Search Feature launched.**
    
    *   View any address’s assets directly on PizzaSwap
        
    *   Explore detailed transaction history for full transparency
        
    *   [Tweet Link](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1918572068313997816)

# brc20-swap Early Access | UniSat

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/community/events/brc20-swap-early-access#the-criteria)

the criteria

*   Active community members who have traded at least 1 BTC on the UniSat Marketplace between July 16th and September 20th
    
*   Active community members who have accumulated at least 500 UniSat Points through UniSat Inscribe between July 16th and September 20th
    
*   OG PASS holders (at block height 808,559)

# UniSat OG Pass Collection | UniSat

The UniSat OG pass is a commemorative card distributed for free to early supporters. It currently grants the following benefits:

*   A 15% reduction in UniSat Inscribing service fees.
    
*   A 25% reduction in UniSat Marketplace service fees.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.unisat.io/community/events/unisat-og-pass-collection#total-supply-189)
